5097      /**
5098       * <i><l>Parser</l> configuration property:&emsp;</i>  Debug output lines.
5099       *
5100       * <p>
5101       * When parse errors occur, this specifies the number of lines of input before and after the
5102       * error location to be printed as part of the exception message.
5103       *
5104       * <h5 class='section'>Example:</h5>
5105       * <p class='bjava'>
5106       *    <jc>// Create a parser whose exceptions print out 100 lines before and after the parse error location.</jc>
5107       *    RestClient <jv>client</jv> = RestClient
5108       *       .<jsm>create</jsm>()
5109       *       .json()
5110       *       .debug()  <jc>// Enable debug mode to capture Reader contents as strings.</jc>
5111       *       .debugOuputLines(100)
5112       *       .build();
5113       *
5114       *    <jc>// Try to parse some bad JSON.</jc>
5115       *    <jk>try</jk> {
5116       *       <jv>client</jv>
5117       *          .get(<js>"/pathToBadJson"</js>)
5118       *          .run()
5119       *          .getContent().as(Object.<jk>class</jk>);  <jc>// Try to parse it.</jc>
5120       *    } <jk>catch</jk> (RestCallException <jv>e</jv>) {
5121       *       System.<jsf>err</jsf>.println(<jv>e</jv>.getMessage());  <jc>// Will display 200 lines of the output.</jc>
5122       *    }
5123       * </p>
5124       *
5125       * <ul class='seealso'>
5126       *    <li class='jm'>{@link org.apache.juneau.parser.Parser.Builder#debugOutputLines(int)}
5127       * </ul>
5128       *
5129       * @param value
5130       *    The new value for this property.
5131       *    <br>The default value is <c>5</c>.
5132       * @return This object.
5133       */
5134      @FluentSetter
5135      public Builder debugOutputLines(int value) {
5136         parsers().forEach(x -> x.debugOutputLines(value));
5137         return this;
5138      }
5139
5140      /**
5141       * <i><l>Parser</l> configuration property:&emsp;</i>  Strict mode.
5142       *
5143       * <p>
5144       * When enabled, strict mode for the parser is enabled.
5145       *
5146       * <p>
5147       * Strict mode can mean different things for different parsers.
5148       *
5149       * <table class='styled'>
5150       *    <tr><th>Parser class</th><th>Strict behavior</th></tr>
5151       *    <tr>
5152       *       <td>All reader-based parsers</td>
5153       *       <td>
5154       *          When enabled, throws {@link ParseException ParseExceptions} on malformed charset input.
5155       *          Otherwise, malformed input is ignored.
5156       *       </td>
5157       *    </tr>
5158       *    <tr>
5159       *       <td>{@link JsonParser}</td>
5160       *       <td>
5161       *          When enabled, throws exceptions on the following invalid JSON syntax:
5162       *          <ul>
5163       *             <li>Unquoted attributes.
5164       *             <li>Missing attribute values.
5165       *             <li>Concatenated strings.
5166       *             <li>Javascript comments.
5167       *             <li>Numbers and booleans when Strings are expected.
5168       *             <li>Numbers valid in Java but not JSON (e.g. octal notation, etc...)
5169       *          </ul>
5170       *       </td>
5171       *    </tr>
5172       * </table>
5173       *
5174       * <h5 class='section'>Example:</h5>
5175       * <p class='bjava'>
5176       *    <jc>// Create a REST client with JSON parser using strict mode.</jc>
5177       *    RestClient <jv>client</jv> = RestClient
5178       *       .<jsm>create</jsm>()
5179       *       .json()
5180       *       .strict()
5181       *       .build();
5182       *
5183       *    <jc>// Try to parse some bad JSON.</jc>
5184       *    <jk>try</jk> {
5185       *       <jv>client</jv>
5186       *          .get(<js>"/pathToBadJson"</js>)
5187       *          .run()
5188       *          .getContent().as(Object.<jk>class</jk>);  <jc>// Try to parse it.</jc>
5189       *    } <jk>catch</jk> (RestCallException <jv>e</jv>) {
5190       *       <jc>// Handle exception.</jc>
5191       *    }
5192       * </p>
5193       *
5194       * <ul class='seealso'>
5195       *    <li class='jm'>{@link org.apache.juneau.parser.Parser.Builder#strict()}
5196       * </ul>
5197       *
5198       * @return This object.
5199       */
5200      @FluentSetter
5201      public Builder strict() {
5202         parsers().forEach(x -> x.strict());
5203         return this;
5204      }
5205
5206      /**
5207       * <i><l>Parser</l> configuration property:&emsp;</i>  Trim parsed strings.
5208       *
5209       * <p>
5210       * When enabled, string values will be trimmed of whitespace using {@link String#trim()} before being added to
5211       * the POJO.
5212       *
5213       * <h5 class='section'>Example:</h5>
5214       * <p class='bjava'>
5215       *    <jc>// Create a REST client with JSON parser with trim-strings enabled.</jc>
5216       *    RestClient <jv>client</jv> = RestClient
5217       *       .<jsm>create</jsm>()
5218       *       .json()
5219       *       .trimStringsOnRead()
5220       *       .build();
5221       *
5222       *    <jc>// Try to parse JSON containing {" foo ":" bar "}.</jc>
5223       *    Map&lt;String,String&gt; <jv>map</jv> = <jv>client</jv>
5224       *       .get(<js>"/pathToJson"</js>)
5225       *       .run()
5226       *       .getContent().as(HashMap.<jk>class</jk>, String.<jk>class</jk>, String.<jk>class</jk>);
5227       *
5228       *    <jc>// Make sure strings are trimmed.</jc>
5229       *    <jsm>assertEquals</jsm>(<js>"bar"</js>, <jv>map</jv>.get(<js>"foo"</js>));
5230       * </p>
5231       *
5232       * <ul class='seealso'>
5233       *    <li class='jm'>{@link org.apache.juneau.parser.Parser.Builder#trimStrings()}
5234       * </ul>
5235       *
5236       * @return This object.
5237       */
5238      @FluentSetter
5239      public Builder trimStringsOnRead() {
5240         parsers().forEach(x -> x.trimStrings());
5241         return this;
5242      }

5256      /**
5257       * <i><l>OpenApiCommon</l> configuration property:&emsp;</i>  Default OpenAPI format for HTTP parts.
5258       *
5259       * <p>
5260       * Specifies the format to use for HTTP parts when not otherwise specified via {@link org.apache.juneau.annotation.Schema#format()} for
5261       * the OpenAPI serializer and parser on this client.
5262       *
5263       * <h5 class='section'>Example:</h5>
5264       * <p class='bjava'>
5265       *    <jc>// Create a REST client with UON part serialization and parsing.</jc>
5266       *    RestClient <jv>client</jv>  = RestClient
5267       *       .<jsm>create</jsm>()
5268       *       .oapiFormat(<jsf>UON</jsf>)
5269       *       .build();
5270       *
5271       *    <jc>// Set a header with a value in UON format.</jc>
5272       *    <jv>client</jv>
5273       *       .get(<js>"/uri"</js>)
5274       *       .header(<js>"Foo"</js>, <js>"bar baz"</js>)  <jc>// Will be serialized as:  'bar baz'</jc>
5275       *       .run();
5276       * </p>
5277       *
5278       * <ul class='values javatree'>
5279       *    <li class='jc'>{@link org.apache.juneau.httppart.HttpPartFormat}
5280       *    <ul>
5281       *       <li class='jf'>{@link org.apache.juneau.httppart.HttpPartFormat#UON UON} - UON notation (e.g. <js>"'foo bar'"</js>).
5282       *       <li class='jf'>{@link org.apache.juneau.httppart.HttpPartFormat#INT32 INT32} - Signed 32 bits.
5283       *       <li class='jf'>{@link org.apache.juneau.httppart.HttpPartFormat#INT64 INT64} - Signed 64 bits.
5284       *       <li class='jf'>{@link org.apache.juneau.httppart.HttpPartFormat#FLOAT FLOAT} - 32-bit floating point number.
5285       *       <li class='jf'>{@link org.apache.juneau.httppart.HttpPartFormat#DOUBLE DOUBLE} - 64-bit floating point number.
5286       *       <li class='jf'>{@link org.apache.juneau.httppart.HttpPartFormat#BYTE BYTE} - BASE-64 encoded characters.
5287       *       <li class='jf'>{@link org.apache.juneau.httppart.HttpPartFormat#BINARY BINARY} - Hexadecimal encoded octets (e.g. <js>"00FF"</js>).
5288       *       <li class='jf'>{@link org.apache.juneau.httppart.HttpPartFormat#BINARY_SPACED BINARY_SPACED} - Spaced-separated hexadecimal encoded octets (e.g. <js>"00 FF"</js>).
5289       *       <li class='jf'>{@link org.apache.juneau.httppart.HttpPartFormat#DATE DATE} - An <a href='http://xml2rfc.ietf.org/public/rfc/html/rfc3339.html#anchor14'>RFC3339 full-date</a>.
5290       *       <li class='jf'>{@link org.apache.juneau.httppart.HttpPartFormat#DATE_TIME DATE_TIME} - An <a href='http://xml2rfc.ietf.org/public/rfc/html/rfc3339.html#anchor14'>RFC3339 date-time</a>.
5291       *       <li class='jf'>{@link org.apache.juneau.httppart.HttpPartFormat#PASSWORD PASSWORD} - Used to hint UIs the input needs to be obscured.
5292       *       <li class='jf'>{@link org.apache.juneau.httppart.HttpPartFormat#NO_FORMAT NO_FORMAT} - (default) Not specified.
5293       *    </ul>
5294       * </ul>
5295       *
5296       * <ul class='seealso'>
5297       *    <li class='jm'>{@link org.apache.juneau.oapi.OpenApiSerializer.Builder#format(HttpPartFormat)}
5298       *    <li class='jm'>{@link org.apache.juneau.oapi.OpenApiParser.Builder#format(HttpPartFormat)}
5299       * </ul>
5300       *
5301       * @param value
5302       *    The new value for this property.
5303       *    <br>The default value is {@link HttpPartFormat#NO_FORMAT}.
5304       * @return This object.
5305       */
5306      @FluentSetter
5307      public Builder oapiFormat(HttpPartFormat value) {
5308         serializers().forEach(OpenApiSerializer.Builder.class, x -> x.format(value));
5309         parsers().forEach(OpenApiParser.Builder.class, x -> x.format(value));
5310         partSerializer().builder(OpenApiSerializer.Builder.class).ifPresent(x -> x.format(value));
5311         partParser().builder(OpenApiParser.Builder.class).ifPresent(x -> x.format(value));
5312         return this;
5313      }

5315      /**
5316       * <i><l>OpenApiCommon</l> configuration property:&emsp;</i>  Default collection format for HTTP parts.
5317       *
5318       * <p>
5319       * Specifies the collection format to use for HTTP parts when not otherwise specified via {@link org.apache.juneau.annotation.Schema#collectionFormat()} for the
5320       * OpenAPI serializer and parser on this client.
5321       *
5322       * <h5 class='section'>Example:</h5>
5323       * <p class='bjava'>
5324       *    <jc>// Create a REST client with CSV format for http parts.</jc>
5325       *    RestClient <jv>client</jv> = RestClient
5326       *       .<jsm>create</jsm>()
5327       *       .collectionFormat(<jsf>CSV</jsf>)
5328       *       .build();
5329       *
5330       *    <jc>// An arbitrary data structure.</jc>
5331       *    AList <jv>list</jv> = AList.<jsm>of</jsm>(
5332       *       <js>"foo"</js>,
5333       *       <js>"bar"</js>,
5334       *       AMap.<jsm>of</jsm>(
5335       *          <js>"baz"</js>, AList.<jsm>of</jsm>(<js>"qux"</js>,<js>"true"</js>,<js>"123"</js>)
5336       *    )
5337       * );
5338       *
5339       *    <jc>// Set a header with a comma-separated list.</jc>
5340       *    <jv>client</jv>
5341       *       .get(<js>"/uri"</js>)
5342       *       .header(<js>"Foo"</js>, <jv>list</jv>)  <jc>// Will be serialized as: foo=bar,baz=qux\,true\,123</jc>
5343       *       .run();
5344       * </p>
5345       *
5346       * <ul class='values javatree'>
5347       *    <li class='jc'>{@link HttpPartCollectionFormat}
5348       *    <ul>
5349       *       <li class='jf'>{@link HttpPartCollectionFormat#CSV CSV} - (default) Comma-separated values (e.g. <js>"foo,bar"</js>).
5350       *       <li class='jf'>{@link HttpPartCollectionFormat#SSV SSV} - Space-separated values (e.g. <js>"foo bar"</js>).
5351       *       <li class='jf'>{@link HttpPartCollectionFormat#TSV TSV} - Tab-separated values (e.g. <js>"foo\tbar"</js>).
5352       *       <li class='jf'>{@link HttpPartCollectionFormat#PIPES PIPES} - Pipe-separated values (e.g. <js>"foo|bar"</js>).
5353       *       <li class='jf'>{@link HttpPartCollectionFormat#MULTI MULTI} - Corresponds to multiple parameter instances instead of multiple values for a single instance (e.g. <js>"foo=bar&amp;foo=baz"</js>).
5354       *       <li class='jf'>{@link HttpPartCollectionFormat#UONC UONC} - UON collection notation (e.g. <js>"@(foo,bar)"</js>).
5355       *    </ul>
5356       * </ul>
5357       *
5358       * <ul class='seealso'>
5359       *    <li class='jm'>{@link org.apache.juneau.oapi.OpenApiSerializer.Builder#collectionFormat(HttpPartCollectionFormat)}
5360       *    <li class='jm'>{@link org.apache.juneau.oapi.OpenApiParser.Builder#collectionFormat(HttpPartCollectionFormat)}
5361       * </ul>
5362       *
5363       * @param value
5364       *    The new value for this property.
5365       *    <br>The default value is {@link HttpPartCollectionFormat#NO_COLLECTION_FORMAT}.
5366       * @return This object.
5367       */
5368      @FluentSetter
5369      public Builder oapiCollectionFormat(HttpPartCollectionFormat value) {
5370         serializers().forEach(OpenApiSerializer.Builder.class, x -> x.collectionFormat(value));
5371         parsers().forEach(OpenApiParser.Builder.class, x -> x.collectionFormat(value));
5372         partSerializer().builder(OpenApiSerializer.Builder.class, x -> x.collectionFormat(value));
5373         partParser().builder(OpenApiParser.Builder.class, x -> x.collectionFormat(value));
5374         return this;
5375      }

5408       *       .run();

5410       *

5412       *    <li class='jf'>{@link ParamFormat#UON} (default) - Use UON notation for parameters.

6504   //-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
6505   // Instance
6506   //-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
6507
6508   final HeaderList.Builder headerData;
6509   final PartList.Builder queryData, formData, pathData;
6510   final CloseableHttpClient httpClient;
6511
6512   private final HttpClientConnectionManager connectionManager;
6513   private final boolean keepHttpClientOpen, detectLeaks, skipEmptyHeaderData, skipEmptyQueryData, skipEmptyFormData;
6514   private final BeanStore beanStore;
6515   private final UrlEncodingSerializer urlEncodingSerializer;  // Used for form posts only.
6516   final HttpPartSerializer partSerializer;
6517   final HttpPartParser partParser;
6518   private final RestCallHandler callHandler;
6519   private final String rootUri;
6520   private volatile boolean isClosed = false;
6521   private final StackTraceElement[] creationStack;
6522   private final Logger logger;
6523   final DetailLevel logRequests;
6524   final BiPredicate<RestRequest,RestResponse> logRequestsPredicate;
6525   final Level logRequestsLevel;
6526   final boolean ignoreErrors;
6527   private final boolean logToConsole;
6528   private final PrintStream console;
6529   private StackTraceElement[] closedStack;
6530   private static final ConcurrentHashMap<Class<?>,Context> requestContexts = new ConcurrentHashMap<>();
6531
6532   // These are read directly by RestCall.
6533   final SerializerSet serializers;
6534   final ParserSet parsers;
6535   Predicate<Integer> errorCodes;
6536
6537   final RestCallInterceptor[] interceptors;
6538
6539   private final Map<Class<?>, HttpPartParser> partParsers = new ConcurrentHashMap<>();
6540   private final Map<Class<?>, HttpPartSerializer> partSerializers = new ConcurrentHashMap<>();
6541
6542   // This is lazy-created.
6543   private volatile ExecutorService executorService;
6544   private final boolean executorServiceShutdownOnClose;
6545
6546   private static final
6547      BiPredicate<RestRequest,RestResponse> LOG_REQUESTS_PREDICATE_DEFAULT = (req,res) -> true;
6548
6549   /**
6550    * Constructor.
6551    *
6552    * @param builder The builder for this client.
6553    */
6554   public RestClient(Builder builder) {
6555      super(builder);
6556
6557      beanStore = builder.beanStore
6558         .addBean(RestClient.class, this);
6559
6560      httpClient = builder.getHttpClient();
6561      headerData = builder.headers().build().copy();
6562      queryData = builder.queryData().build().copy();
6563      formData = builder.formData().build().copy();
6564      pathData = builder.pathData().build().copy();
6565      callHandler = builder.callHandler().run();
6566      skipEmptyHeaderData = builder.skipEmptyHeaderData;
6567      skipEmptyQueryData = builder.skipEmptyQueryData;
6568      skipEmptyFormData = builder.skipEmptyFormData;
6569      rootUri = builder.rootUri;
6570      errorCodes = builder.errorCodes;
6571      connectionManager = builder.connectionManager;
6572      console = builder.console != null ? builder.console : System.err;
6573      executorService = builder.executorService;
6574      executorServiceShutdownOnClose = builder.executorServiceShutdownOnClose;
6575      ignoreErrors = builder.ignoreErrors;
6576      keepHttpClientOpen = builder.keepHttpClientOpen;
6577      detectLeaks = builder.detectLeaks;
6578      logger = builder.logger != null ? builder.logger : Logger.getLogger(RestClient.class.getName());
6579      logToConsole = builder.logToConsole || isDebug();
6580      logRequests = builder.logRequests != null ? builder.logRequests : isDebug() ? DetailLevel.FULL : DetailLevel.NONE;
6581      logRequestsLevel = builder.logRequestsLevel != null ? builder.logRequestsLevel : isDebug() ? Level.WARNING : Level.OFF;
6582      logRequestsPredicate = builder.logRequestsPredicate != null ? builder.logRequestsPredicate : LOG_REQUESTS_PREDICATE_DEFAULT;
6583      interceptors = builder.interceptors != null ? builder.interceptors.toArray(EMPTY_REST_CALL_INTERCEPTORS) : EMPTY_REST_CALL_INTERCEPTORS;
6584      serializers = builder.serializers().build();
6585      parsers = builder.parsers().build();
6586      partSerializer = builder.partSerializer().create();
6587      partParser = builder.partParser().create();
6588      urlEncodingSerializer = builder.urlEncodingSerializer().build();
6589      creationStack = isDebug() ? Thread.currentThread().getStackTrace() : null;
6590   }
6591
6592   @Override /* Context */
6593   public Builder copy() {
6594      throw new NoSuchMethodError("Not implemented.");
6595   }
6596
6597   /**
6598    * Calls {@link CloseableHttpClient#close()} on the underlying {@link CloseableHttpClient}.
6599    *
6600    * <p>
6601    * It's good practice to call this method after the client is no longer used.
6602    *
6603    * @throws IOException Thrown by underlying stream.
6604    */
6605   @Override
6606   public void close() throws IOException {
6607      isClosed = true;
6608      if (! keepHttpClientOpen)
6609         httpClient.close();
6610      if (executorService != null && executorServiceShutdownOnClose)
6611         executorService.shutdown();
6612      if (creationStack != null)
6613         closedStack = Thread.currentThread().getStackTrace();
6614   }
6615
6616   /**
6617    * Same as {@link #close()}, but ignores any exceptions.
6618    */
6619   public void closeQuietly() {
6620      isClosed = true;
6621      try {
6622         if (! keepHttpClientOpen)
6623            httpClient.close();
6624         if (executorService != null && executorServiceShutdownOnClose)
6625            executorService.shutdown();
6626      } catch (Throwable t) {}
6627      if (creationStack != null)
6628         closedStack = Thread.currentThread().getStackTrace();
6629   }
6630
6631   /**
6632    * Entrypoint for executing all requests and returning a response.
6633    *
6634    * <p>
6635    * Subclasses can override this method to provide specialized handling.
6636    *
6637    * <p>
6638    * The behavior of this method can also be modified by specifying a different {@link RestCallHandler}.
6639    *
6640    * <ul class='seealso'>
6641    *    <li class='jm'>{@link Builder#callHandler()}
6642    * </ul>
6643    *
6644    * @param target The target host for the request.
6645    *    <br>Implementations may accept <jk>null</jk> if they can still determine a route, for example to a default
6646    *       target or by inspecting the request.
6647    * @param request The request to execute.
6648    * @param context The context to use for the execution, or <jk>null</jk> to use the default context.
6649    * @return
6650    *    The response to the request.
6651    *    <br>This is always a final response, never an intermediate response with an 1xx status code.
6652    *    <br>Whether redirects or authentication challenges will be returned or handled automatically depends on the
6653    *       implementation and configuration of this client.
6654    * @throws IOException In case of a problem or the connection was aborted.
6655    * @throws ClientProtocolException In case of an http protocol error.
6656    */
6657   @Override /* RestCallHandler */
6658   public HttpResponse run(HttpHost target, HttpRequest request, HttpContext context) throws ClientProtocolException, IOException {
6659      return callHandler.run(target, request, context);
6660   }
6661
6662   /**
6663    * Perform a <c>GET</c> request against the specified URI.
6664    *
6665    * @param uri
6666    *    The URI of the remote REST resource.
6667    *    <br>Can be any of the following types:
6668    *    <ul>
6669    *       <li>{@link URIBuilder}
6670    *       <li>{@link URI}
6671    *       <li>{@link URL}
6672    *       <li>{@link String}
6673    *       <li>{@link Object} - Converted to <c>String</c> using <c>toString()</c>
6674    *    </ul>
6675    * @return
6676    *    A {@link RestRequest} object that can be further tailored before executing the request and getting the response
6677    *    as a parsed object.
6678    * @throws RestCallException If any authentication errors occurred.
6679    */
6680   public RestRequest get(Object uri) throws RestCallException {
6681      return request(op("GET", uri, NO_BODY));
6682   }
6683
6684   /**
6685    * Perform a <c>GET</c> request against the root URI.
6686    *
6687    * @return
6688    *    A {@link RestRequest} object that can be further tailored before executing the request and getting the response
6689    *    as a parsed object.
6690    * @throws RestCallException If any authentication errors occurred.
6691    */
6692   public RestRequest get() throws RestCallException {
6693      return request(op("GET", null, NO_BODY));
6694   }
6695
6696   /**
6697    * Perform a <c>PUT</c> request against the specified URI.
6698    *
6699    * @param uri
6700    *    The URI of the remote REST resource.
6701    *    <br>Can be any of the following types:
6702    *    <ul>
6703    *       <li>{@link URIBuilder}
6704    *       <li>{@link URI}
6705    *       <li>{@link URL}
6706    *       <li>{@link String}
6707    *       <li>{@link Object} - Converted to <c>String</c> using <c>toString()</c>
6708    *    </ul>
6709    * @param body
6710    *    The object to serialize and transmit to the URI as the body of the request.
6711    *    Can be of the following types:
6712    *    <ul class='spaced-list'>
6713    *       <li>
6714    *          {@link Reader} - Raw contents of {@code Reader} will be serialized to remote resource.
6715    *       <li>
6716    *          {@link InputStream} - Raw contents of {@code InputStream} will be serialized to remote resource.
6717    *       <li>
6718    *          {@link Object} - POJO to be converted to text using the {@link Serializer} registered with the
6719    *          {@link RestClient}.
6720    *       <li>
6721    *          {@link HttpEntity} / {@link HttpResource} - Bypass Juneau serialization and pass HttpEntity directly to HttpClient.
6722    *       <li>
6723    *          {@link PartList} - Converted to a URL-encoded FORM post.
6724    *       <li>
6725    *          {@link Supplier} - A supplier of anything on this list.
6726    *    </ul>
6727    * @return
6728    *    A {@link RestRequest} object that can be further tailored before executing the request
6729    *    and getting the response as a parsed object.
6730    * @throws RestCallException If any authentication errors occurred.
6731    */
6732   public RestRequest put(Object uri, Object body) throws RestCallException {
6733      return request(op("PUT", uri, body));
6734   }
6735
6736   /**
6737    * Perform a <c>PUT</c> request against the specified URI using a plain text body bypassing the serializer.
6738    *
6739    * @param uri
6740    *    The URI of the remote REST resource.
6741    *    <br>Can be any of the following types:
6742    *    <ul>
6743    *       <li>{@link URIBuilder}
6744    *       <li>{@link URI}
6745    *       <li>{@link URL}
6746    *       <li>{@link String}
6747    *       <li>{@link Object} - Converted to <c>String</c> using <c>toString()</c>
6748    *    </ul>
6749    * @param body
6750    *    The object to serialize and transmit to the URI as the body of the request bypassing the serializer.
6751    * @param contentType The content type of the request.
6752    * @return
6753    *    A {@link RestRequest} object that can be further tailored before executing the request
6754    *    and getting the response as a parsed object.
6755    * @throws RestCallException If any authentication errors occurred.
6756    */
6757   public RestRequest put(Object uri, String body, ContentType contentType) throws RestCallException {
6758      return request(op("PUT", uri, stringBody(body))).header(contentType);
6759   }
6760
6761   /**
6762    * Same as {@link #put(Object, Object)} but don't specify the input yet.
6763    *

6795    *    The URI of the remote REST resource.

6797    *    <ul>
6798    *       <li>{@link URIBuilder}
6799    *       <li>{@link URI}
6800    *       <li>{@link URL}
6801    *       <li>{@link String}
6802    *       <li>{@link Object} - Converted to <c>String</c> using <c>toString()</c>
6803    *    </ul>
6804    * @param body
6805    *    The object to serialize and transmit to the URI as the body of the request.
6806    *    Can be of the following types:
6807    *    <ul class='spaced-list'>
6808    *       <li>
6809    *          {@link Reader} - Raw contents of {@code Reader} will be serialized to remote resource.
6810    *       <li>
6811    *          {@link InputStream} - Raw contents of {@code InputStream} will be serialized to remote resource.

6814    *          {@link RestClient}.

6819    *       <li>
6820    *          {@link Supplier} - A supplier of anything on this list.
6821    *    </ul>

6823    *    A {@link RestRequest} object that can be further tailored before executing the request and getting the response
6824    *    as a parsed object.

6953   /**
6954    * Perform a <c>POST</c> request with a content type of <c>application/x-www-form-urlencoded</c>
6955    * against the specified URI.
6956    *
6957    * @param uri
6958    *    The URI of the remote REST resource.
6959    *    <br>Can be any of the following types:
6960    *    <ul>
6961    *       <li>{@link URIBuilder}
6962    *       <li>{@link URI}
6963    *       <li>{@link URL}
6964    *       <li>{@link String}
6965    *       <li>{@link Object} - Converted to <c>String</c> using <c>toString()</c>
6966    *    </ul>
6967    * @param body
6968    *    The object to serialize and transmit to the URI as the body of the request.
6969    *    <ul class='spaced-list'>
6970    *       <li>{@link NameValuePair} - URL-encoded as a single name-value pair.
6971    *       <li>{@link NameValuePair} array - URL-encoded as name value pairs.
6972    *       <li>{@link PartList} - URL-encoded as name value pairs.
6973    *       <li>{@link Reader}/{@link InputStream}- Streamed directly and <l>Content-Type</l> set to <js>"application/x-www-form-urlencoded"</js>
6974    *       <li>{@link HttpResource} - Raw contents will be serialized to remote resource.  Additional headers and media type will be set on request.
6975    *       <li>{@link HttpEntity} - Bypass Juneau serialization and pass HttpEntity directly to HttpClient.
6976    *       <li>{@link Object} - Converted to a {@link SerializedEntity} using {@link UrlEncodingSerializer} to serialize.
6977    *       <li>{@link Supplier} - A supplier of anything on this list.
6978    *    </ul>
6979    * @return
6980    *    A {@link RestRequest} object that can be further tailored before executing the request and getting the response
6981    *    as a parsed object.
6982    * @throws RestCallException If any authentication errors occurred.
6983    */
6984   public RestRequest formPost(Object uri, Object body) throws RestCallException {
6985      RestRequest req = request(op("POST", uri, NO_BODY));
6986      try {
6987         if (body instanceof Supplier)
6988            body = ((Supplier<?>)body).get();
6989         if (body instanceof NameValuePair)
6990            return req.content(new UrlEncodedFormEntity(alist((NameValuePair)body)));
6991         if (body instanceof NameValuePair[])
6992            return req.content(new UrlEncodedFormEntity(alist((NameValuePair[])body)));
6993         if (body instanceof PartList)
6994            return req.content(new UrlEncodedFormEntity(((PartList)body).toNameValuePairs()));
6995         if (body instanceof HttpResource)
6996            ((HttpResource)body).getHeaders().forEach(x-> req.header(x));
6997         if (body instanceof HttpEntity) {
6998            HttpEntity e = (HttpEntity)body;
6999            if (e.getContentType() == null)
7000               req.header(ContentType.APPLICATION_FORM_URLENCODED);
7001            return req.content(e);
7002         }
7003         if (body instanceof Reader || body instanceof InputStream)
7004            return req.header(ContentType.APPLICATION_FORM_URLENCODED).content(body);
7005         return req.content(serializedEntity(body, urlEncodingSerializer, null).build());
7006      } catch (IOException e) {
7007         throw new RestCallException(null, e, "Could not read form post body.");
7008      }
7009   }

7153
7154   /**
7155    * Performs a REST call where the entire call is specified in a simple string.
7156    *
7157    * <p>
7158    * This method is useful for performing callbacks when the target of a callback is passed in
7159    * on an initial request, for example to signal when a long-running process has completed.
7160    *
7161    * <p>
7162    * The call string can be any of the following formats:
7163    * <ul class='spaced-list'>
7164    *    <li>
7165    *       <js>"[method] [uri]"</js> - e.g. <js>"GET http://localhost/callback"</js>
7166    *    <li>
7167    *       <js>"[method] [uri] [payload]"</js> - e.g. <js>"POST http://localhost/callback some text payload"</js>
7168    *    <li>
7169    *       <js>"[method] [headers] [uri] [payload]"</js> - e.g. <js>"POST {'Content-Type':'text/json'} http://localhost/callback {'some':'json'}"</js>
7170    * </ul>
7171    * <p>
7172    * The payload will always be sent using a simple {@link StringEntity}.
7173    *
7174    * @param callString The call string.
7175    * @return
7176    *    A {@link RestRequest} object that can be further tailored before executing the request and getting the response
7177    *    as a parsed object.
7178    * @throws RestCallException REST call failed.
7179    */
7180   public RestRequest callback(String callString) throws RestCallException {
7181      callString = emptyIfNull(callString);
7182
7183      // S01 - Looking for end of method.
7184      // S02 - Found end of method, looking for beginning of URI or headers.
7185      // S03 - Found beginning of headers, looking for end of headers.
7186      // S04 - Found end of headers, looking for beginning of URI.
7187      // S05 - Found beginning of URI, looking for end of URI.
7188
7189      StateMachineState state = S01;
7190
7191      int mark = 0;
7192      String method = null, headers = null, uri = null, content = null;
7193      for (int i = 0; i < callString.length(); i++) {
7194         char c = callString.charAt(i);
7195         if (state == S01) {
7196            if (isWhitespace(c)) {
7197               method = callString.substring(mark, i);
7198               state = S02;
7199            }
7200         } else if (state == S02) {
7201            if (! isWhitespace(c)) {
7202               mark = i;
7203               if (c == '{')
7204                  state = S03;
7205               else
7206                  state = S05;
7207            }
7208         } else if (state == S03) {
7209            if (c == '}') {
7210               headers = callString.substring(mark, i+1);
7211               state = S04;
7212            }
7213         } else if (state == S04) {
7214            if (! isWhitespace(c)) {
7215               mark = i;
7216               state = S05;
7217            }
7218         } else /* (state == S05) */ {
7219            if (isWhitespace(c)) {
7220               uri = callString.substring(mark, i);
7221               content = callString.substring(i).trim();
7222               break;
7223            }
7224         }
7225      }
7226
7227      if (state != S05)
7228         throw new RestCallException(null, null, "Invalid format for call string.  State={0}", state);
7229
7230      try {
7231         RestRequest req = request(method, uri, isNotEmpty(content));
7232         if (headers != null)
7233            JsonMap.ofJson(headers).forEach((k,v) -> req.header(stringHeader(k, stringify(v))));
7234         if (isNotEmpty(content))
7235            req.contentString(content);
7236         return req;
7237      } catch (ParseException e) {
7238         throw new RestCallException(null, e, "Invalid format for call string.");
7239      }
7240   }
7241
7242   /**
7243    * Perform a generic REST call.
7244    *
7245    * @param method The HTTP method.
7246    * @param uri
7247    *    The URI of the remote REST resource.
7248    *    <br>Can be any of the following types:
7249    *    <ul>
7250    *       <li>{@link URIBuilder}
7251    *       <li>{@link URI}
7252    *       <li>{@link URL}
7253    *       <li>{@link String}
7254    *       <li>{@link Object} - Converted to <c>String</c> using <c>toString()</c>
7255    *    </ul>
7256    * @param body
7257    *    The HTTP body content.
7258    *    Can be of the following types:
7259    *    <ul class='spaced-list'>
7260    *       <li>
7261    *          {@link Reader} - Raw contents of {@code Reader} will be serialized to remote resource.
7262    *       <li>
7263    *          {@link InputStream} - Raw contents of {@code InputStream} will be serialized to remote resource.
7264    *       <li>
7265    *          {@link HttpResource} - Raw contents will be serialized to remote resource.  Additional headers and media type will be set on request.
7266    *       <li>
7267    *          {@link HttpEntity} - Bypass Juneau serialization and pass HttpEntity directly to HttpClient.
7268    *       <li>
7269    *          {@link Object} - POJO to be converted to text using the {@link Serializer} registered with the
7270    *          {@link RestClient}.
7271    *       <li>
7272    *          {@link PartList} - Converted to a URL-encoded FORM post.
7273    *       <li>
7274    *          {@link Supplier} - A supplier of anything on this list.
7275    *    </ul>
7276    *    This parameter is IGNORED if the method type normally does not have content.
7277    * @return
7278    *    A {@link RestRequest} object that can be further tailored before executing the request and getting the response
7279    *    as a parsed object.
7280    * @throws RestCallException If any authentication errors occurred.
7281    */
7282   public RestRequest request(String method, Object uri, Object body) throws RestCallException {

7309   /**
7310    * Perform a generic REST call.
7311    *
7312    * <p>
7313    * Typically you're going to use {@link #request(String, Object)} or {@link #request(String, Object, Object)},
7314    * but this method is provided to allow you to perform non-standard HTTP methods (e.g. HTTP FOO).
7315    *
7316    * @param method The method name (e.g. <js>"GET"</js>, <js>"OPTIONS"</js>).
7317    * @param uri
7318    *    The URI of the remote REST resource.
7319    *    <br>Can be any of the following types:
7320    *    <ul>
7321    *       <li>{@link URIBuilder}
7322    *       <li>{@link URI}
7323    *       <li>{@link URL}
7324    *       <li>{@link String}
7325    *       <li>{@link Object} - Converted to <c>String</c> using <c>toString()</c>
7326    *    </ul>
7327    * @param hasBody Boolean flag indicating if the specified request has content associated with it.
7328    * @return
7329    *    A {@link RestRequest} object that can be further tailored before executing the request and getting the response
7330    *    as a parsed object.
7331    * @throws RestCallException If any authentication errors occurred.
7332    */
7333   public RestRequest request(String method, Object uri, boolean hasBody) throws RestCallException {
7334      return request(op(method, uri, NO_BODY).hasContent(hasBody));
7335   }
7336
7337   /**
7338    * Perform an arbitrary request against the specified URI.
7339    *
7340    * @param op The operation that identifies the HTTP method, URL, and optional payload.
7341    * @return
7342    *    A {@link RestRequest} object that can be further tailored before executing the request and getting the response
7343    *    as a parsed object.
7344    * @throws RestCallException If any authentication errors occurred.
7345    */
7346   public RestRequest request(RestOperation op) throws RestCallException {
7347      if (isClosed) {
7348         Exception e2 = null;
7349         if (closedStack != null) {
7350            e2 = new Exception("Creation stack:");
7351            e2.setStackTrace(closedStack);
7352            throw new RestCallException(null, e2, "RestClient.close() has already been called.  This client cannot be reused.");
7353         }
7354         throw new RestCallException(null, null, "RestClient.close() has already been called.  This client cannot be reused.  Closed location stack trace can be displayed by setting the system property 'org.apache.juneau.rest.client2.RestClient.trackCreation' to true.");
7355      }
7356
7357      RestRequest req = createRequest(toURI(op.getUri(), rootUri), op.getMethod(), op.hasContent());
7358
7359      onInit(req);
7360
7361      req.content(op.getContent());
7362
7363      return req;
7364   }

7367    * Creates a {@link RestRequest} object from the specified {@link HttpRequest} object.

7371    *
7372    * @param uri The target.
7373    * @param method The HTTP method (uppercase).
7374    * @param hasBody Whether this method has a request entity.
7375    * @return A new {@link RestRequest} object.
7376    * @throws RestCallException If an exception or non-200 response code occurred during the connection attempt.
7377    */
7378   protected RestRequest createRequest(URI uri, String method, boolean hasBody) throws RestCallException {
7379      return new RestRequest(this, uri, method, hasBody);
7380   }

7399   /**
7400    * Create a new proxy interface against a 3rd-party REST interface.
7401    *
7402    * <p>
7403    * The URI to the REST interface is based on the following values:
7404    * <ul>
7405    *    <li>The {@link Remote#path() @Remote(path)} annotation on the interface (<c>remote-path</c>).
7406    *    <li>The {@link Builder#rootUri(Object) rootUri} on the client (<c>root-url</c>).
7407    *    <li>The fully-qualified class name of the interface (<c>class-name</c>).
7408    * </ul>
7409    *
7410    * <p>
7411    * The URI calculation is as follows:
7412    * <ul>
7413    *    <li><c>remote-path</c> - If remote path is absolute.
7414    *    <li><c>root-uri/remote-path</c> - If remote path is relative and root-uri has been specified.
7415    *    <li><c>root-uri/class-name</c> - If remote path is not specified.
7416    * </ul>
7417    *
7418    * <p>
7419    * If the information is not available to resolve to an absolute URI, a {@link RemoteMetadataException} is thrown.
7420    *
7421    * <h5 class='section'>Examples:</h5>
7422    * <p class='bjava'>
7423    *    <jk>package</jk> org.apache.foo;
7424    *
7425    *    <ja>@RemoteResource</ja>(path=<js>"http://hostname/resturi/myinterface1"</js>)
7426    *    <jk>public interface</jk> MyInterface1 { ... }
7427    *
7428    *    <ja>@RemoteResource</ja>(path=<js>"/myinterface2"</js>)
7429    *    <jk>public interface</jk> MyInterface2 { ... }
7430    *
7431    *    <jk>public interface</jk> MyInterface3 { ... }
7432    *
7433    *    <jc>// Resolves to "http://localhost/resturi/myinterface1"</jc>
7434    *    MyInterface1 <jv>interface1</jv> = RestClient
7435    *       .<jsm>create</jsm>()
7436    *       .build()
7437    *       .getRemote(MyInterface1.<jk>class</jk>);
7438    *
7439    *    <jc>// Resolves to "http://hostname/resturi/myinterface2"</jc>
7440    *    MyInterface2 <jv>interface2</jv> = RestClient
7441    *       .<jsm>create</jsm>()
7442    *       .rootUri(<js>"http://hostname/resturi"</js>)
7443    *       .build()
7444    *       .getRemote(MyInterface2.<jk>class</jk>);
7445    *
7446    *    <jc>// Resolves to "http://hostname/resturi/org.apache.foo.MyInterface3"</jc>
7447    *    MyInterface3 <jv>interface3</jv> = RestClient
7448    *       .<jsm>create</jsm>()
7449    *       .rootUri(<js>"http://hostname/resturi"</js>)
7450    *       .build()
7451    *       .getRemote(MyInterface3.<jk>class</jk>);
7452    * </p>
7453    *
7454    * <ul class='notes'>
7455    *    <li class='note'>
7456    *       If you plan on using your proxy in a multi-threaded environment, you'll want to use an underlying
7457    *       pooling client connection manager.
7458    * </ul>
7459    *
7460    * <ul class='seealso'>
7461    *    <li class='link'>{@doc jrc.Proxies}
7462    * </ul>
7463    *
7464    * @param <T> The interface to create a proxy for.
7465    * @param interfaceClass The interface to create a proxy for.
7466    * @return The new proxy interface.
7467    * @throws RemoteMetadataException If the REST URI cannot be determined based on the information given.
7468    */
7469   public <T> T getRemote(Class<T> interfaceClass) {
7470      return getRemote(interfaceClass, null);
7471   }
7472
7473   /**
7474    * Same as {@link #getRemote(Class)} except explicitly specifies the URI of the REST interface.
7475    *
7476    * <ul class='seealso'>
7477    *    <li class='link'>{@doc jrc.Proxies}
7478    * </ul>
7479    *
7480    * @param <T> The interface to create a proxy for.
7481    * @param interfaceClass The interface to create a proxy for.
7482    * @param rootUri The URI of the REST interface.
7483    * @return The new proxy interface.
7484    */
7485   public <T> T getRemote(Class<T> interfaceClass, Object rootUri) {
7486      return getRemote(interfaceClass, rootUri, null, null);
7487   }

7489   /**
7490    * Same as {@link #getRemote(Class, Object)} but allows you to override the serializer and parser used.
7491    *
7492    * <ul class='seealso'>
7493    *    <li class='link'>{@doc jrc.Proxies}
7494    * </ul>
7495
7496    * @param <T> The interface to create a proxy for.
7497    * @param interfaceClass The interface to create a proxy for.
7498    * @param rootUri The URI of the REST interface.
7499    * @param serializer The serializer used to serialize POJOs to the body of the HTTP request.
7500    * @param parser The parser used to parse POJOs from the body of the HTTP response.
7501    * @return The new proxy interface.
7502    */
7503   @SuppressWarnings({ "unchecked" })
7504   public <T> T getRemote(final Class<T> interfaceClass, Object rootUri, final Serializer serializer, final Parser parser) {
7505
7506      if (rootUri == null)
7507         rootUri = this.rootUri;
7508
7509      final String restUrl2 = trimSlashes(emptyIfNull(rootUri));
7510
7511      return (T)Proxy.newProxyInstance(
7512         interfaceClass.getClassLoader(),
7513         new Class[] { interfaceClass },
7514         new InvocationHandler() {
7515
7516            final RemoteMeta rm = new RemoteMeta(interfaceClass);
7517
7518            @Override /* InvocationHandler */
7519            public Object invoke(Object proxy, Method method, Object[] args) throws Throwable {
7520               RemoteOperationMeta rom = rm.getOperationMeta(method);
7521
7522               String uri = rom.getFullPath();
7523               if (uri.indexOf("://") == -1)
7524                  uri = restUrl2 + '/' + uri;
7525               if (uri.indexOf("://") == -1)
7526                  throw new RemoteMetadataException(interfaceClass, "Root URI has not been specified.  Cannot construct absolute path to remote resource.");
7527
7528               String httpMethod = rom.getHttpMethod();
7529               RestRequest rc = request(httpMethod, uri, hasContent(httpMethod));
7530
7531               rc.serializer(serializer);
7532               rc.parser(parser);
7533
7534               rm.getHeaders().forEach(x -> rc.header(x));
7535               rom.forEachPathArg(a -> rc.pathArg(a.getName(), args[a.getIndex()], a.getSchema(), a.getSerializer().orElse(partSerializer)));
7536               rom.forEachQueryArg(a -> rc.queryArg(a.getName(), args[a.getIndex()], a.getSchema(), a.getSerializer().orElse(partSerializer), a.isSkipIfEmpty()));
7537               rom.forEachFormDataArg(a -> rc.formDataArg(a.getName(), args[a.getIndex()], a.getSchema(), a.getSerializer().orElse(partSerializer), a.isSkipIfEmpty()));
7538               rom.forEachHeaderArg(a -> rc.headerArg(a.getName(), args[a.getIndex()], a.getSchema(), a.getSerializer().orElse(partSerializer), a.isSkipIfEmpty()));
7539
7540               RemoteOperationArg ba = rom.getContentArg();
7541               if (ba != null)
7542                  rc.content(args[ba.getIndex()], ba.getSchema());
7543
7544               rom.forEachRequestArg(rmba -> {
7545                     RequestBeanMeta rbm = rmba.getMeta();
7546                     Object bean = args[rmba.getIndex()];
7547                     if (bean != null) {
7548                        for (RequestBeanPropertyMeta p : rbm.getProperties()) {
7549                           Object val = safeSupplier(()->p.getGetter().invoke(bean));
7550                           HttpPartType pt = p.getPartType();
7551                           String pn = p.getPartName();
7552                           HttpPartSchema schema = p.getSchema();
7553                           if (pt == PATH)
7554                              rc.pathArg(pn, val, schema, p.getSerializer().orElse(partSerializer));
7555                           else if (val != null) {
7556                              if (pt == QUERY)
7557                                 rc.queryArg(pn, val, schema, p.getSerializer().orElse(partSerializer), schema.isSkipIfEmpty());
7558                              else if (pt == FORMDATA)
7559                                 rc.formDataArg(pn, val, schema, p.getSerializer().orElse(partSerializer), schema.isSkipIfEmpty());
7560                              else if (pt == HEADER)
7561                                 rc.headerArg(pn, val, schema, p.getSerializer().orElse(partSerializer), schema.isSkipIfEmpty());
7562                              else /* (pt == HttpPartType.BODY) */
7563                                 rc.content(val, schema);
7564                           }
7565                        }
7566                     }
7567               });
7568
7569               RemoteOperationReturn ror = rom.getReturns();
7570               if (ror.isFuture()) {
7571                  return getExecutorService().submit(new Callable<Object>() {
7572                     @Override
7573                     public Object call() throws Exception {
7574                        try {
7575                           return executeRemote(interfaceClass, rc, method, rom);
7576                        } catch (Exception e) {
7577                           throw e;
7578                        } catch (Throwable e) {
7579                           throw runtimeException(e);
7580                        }
7581                     }
7582                  });
7583               } else if (ror.isCompletableFuture()) {
7584                  CompletableFuture<Object> cf = new CompletableFuture<>();
7585                  getExecutorService().submit(new Callable<Object>() {
7586                     @Override
7587                     public Object call() throws Exception {
7588                        try {
7589                           cf.complete(executeRemote(interfaceClass, rc, method, rom));
7590                        } catch (Throwable e) {
7591                           cf.completeExceptionally(e);
7592                        }
7593                        return null;
7594                     }
7595                  });
7596                  return cf;
7597               }
7598
7599               return executeRemote(interfaceClass, rc, method, rom);
7600            }
7601      });
7602   }
7603
7604   Object executeRemote(Class<?> interfaceClass, RestRequest rc, Method method, RemoteOperationMeta rom) throws Throwable {
7605      RemoteOperationReturn ror = rom.getReturns();
7606
7607      try {
7608         Object ret = null;
7609         RestResponse res = null;
7610         rc.rethrow(RuntimeException.class);
7611         rom.forEachException(x -> rc.rethrow(x));
7612         if (ror.getReturnValue() == RemoteReturn.NONE) {
7613            res = rc.complete();
7614         } else if (ror.getReturnValue() == RemoteReturn.STATUS) {
7615            res = rc.complete();
7616            int returnCode = res.getStatusCode();
7617            Class<?> rt = method.getReturnType();
7618            if (rt == Integer.class || rt == int.class)
7619               ret = returnCode;
7620            else if (rt == Boolean.class || rt == boolean.class)
7621               ret = returnCode < 400;
7622            else
7623               throw new RestCallException(res, null, "Invalid return type on method annotated with @RemoteOp(returns=RemoteReturn.STATUS).  Only integer and booleans types are valid.");
7624         } else if (ror.getReturnValue() == RemoteReturn.BEAN) {
7625            rc.ignoreErrors();
7626            res = rc.run();
7627            ret = res.as(ror.getResponseBeanMeta());
7628         } else {
7629            Class<?> rt = method.getReturnType();
7630            if (Throwable.class.isAssignableFrom(rt))
7631               rc.ignoreErrors();
7632            res = rc.run();
7633            Object v = res.getContent().as(ror.getReturnType());
7634            if (v == null && rt.isPrimitive())
7635               v = ClassInfo.of(rt).getPrimitiveDefault();
7636            ret = v;
7637         }
7638         return ret;
7639      } catch (RestCallException e) {
7640         Throwable t = e.getCause();
7641         if (t instanceof RuntimeException)
7642            throw t;
7643         for (Class<?> t2 : method.getExceptionTypes())
7644            if (t2.isInstance(t))
7645               throw t;
7646         throw runtimeException(e);
7647      }
7648   }

7650   /**
7651    * Create a new proxy interface against an RRPC-style service.
7652    *
7653    * <p>
7654    * Remote interfaces are interfaces exposed on the server side using either the <c>RrpcServlet</c>
7655    * or <c>RRPC</c> REST methods.
7656    *
7657    * <p>
7658    * The URI to the REST interface is based on the following values:
7659    * <ul>
7660    *    <li>The {@link Remote#path() @Remote(path)} annotation on the interface (<c>remote-path</c>).
7661    *    <li>The {@link Builder#rootUri(Object) rootUri} on the client (<c>root-url</c>).
7662    *    <li>The fully-qualified class name of the interface (<c>class-name</c>).
7663    * </ul>
7664    *
7665    * <p>
7666    * The URI calculation is as follows:
7667    * <ul>
7668    *    <li><c>remote-path</c> - If remote path is absolute.
7669    *    <li><c>root-url/remote-path</c> - If remote path is relative and root-url has been specified.
7670    *    <li><c>root-url/class-name</c> - If remote path is not specified.
7671    * </ul>
7672    *
7673    * <p>
7674    * If the information is not available to resolve to an absolute URI, a {@link RemoteMetadataException} is thrown.
7675    *
7676    * <ul class='notes'>
7677    *    <li class='note'>
7678    *       If you plan on using your proxy in a multi-threaded environment, you'll want to use an underlying
7679    *       pooling client connection manager.
7680    * </ul>
7681    *
7682    * <ul class='seealso'>
7683    *    <li class='link'>{@doc jrs.RestRpc}
7684    * </ul>
7685    *
7686    * @param <T> The interface to create a proxy for.
7687    * @param interfaceClass The interface to create a proxy for.
7688    * @return The new proxy interface.
7689    * @throws RemoteMetadataException If the REST URI cannot be determined based on the information given.
7690    */
7691   public <T> T getRrpcInterface(final Class<T> interfaceClass) {
7692      return getRrpcInterface(interfaceClass, null);
7693   }

7695   /**
7696    * Same as {@link #getRrpcInterface(Class)} except explicitly specifies the URI of the REST interface.
7697    *
7698    * <ul class='seealso'>
7699    *    <li class='link'>{@doc jrs.RestRpc}
7700    * </ul>
7701    *
7702    * @param <T> The interface to create a proxy for.
7703    * @param interfaceClass The interface to create a proxy for.
7704    * @param uri The URI of the REST interface.
7705    * @return The new proxy interface.
7706    */
7707   public <T> T getRrpcInterface(final Class<T> interfaceClass, final Object uri) {
7708      return getRrpcInterface(interfaceClass, uri, null, null);

7711   /**
7712    * Same as {@link #getRrpcInterface(Class, Object)} but allows you to override the serializer and parser used.
7713    *
7714    * <ul class='seealso'>
7715    *    <li class='link'>{@doc jrs.RestRpc}
7716    * </ul>
7717    *
7718    * @param <T> The interface to create a proxy for.
7719    * @param interfaceClass The interface to create a proxy for.
7720    * @param uri The URI of the REST interface.
7721    * @param serializer The serializer used to serialize POJOs to the body of the HTTP request.
7722    * @param parser The parser used to parse POJOs from the body of the HTTP response.
7723    * @return The new proxy interface.
7724    */
7725   @SuppressWarnings({ "unchecked" })
7726   public <T> T getRrpcInterface(final Class<T> interfaceClass, Object uri, final Serializer serializer, final Parser parser) {
7727
7728      if (uri == null) {
7729         RrpcInterfaceMeta rm = new RrpcInterfaceMeta(interfaceClass, "");
7730         String path = rm.getPath();
7731         if (path.indexOf("://") == -1) {
7732            if (isEmpty(rootUri))
7733               throw new RemoteMetadataException(interfaceClass, "Root URI has not been specified.  Cannot construct absolute path to remote interface.");
7734            path = trimSlashes(rootUri) + '/' + path;
7735         }
7736         uri = path;
7737      }
7738
7739      final String restUrl2 = stringify(uri);
7740
7741      return (T)Proxy.newProxyInstance(
7742         interfaceClass.getClassLoader(),
7743         new Class[] { interfaceClass },
7744         new InvocationHandler() {
7745
7746            final RrpcInterfaceMeta rm = new RrpcInterfaceMeta(interfaceClass, restUrl2);
7747
7748            @Override /* InvocationHandler */
7749            public Object invoke(Object proxy, Method method, Object[] args) throws Throwable {
7750               RrpcInterfaceMethodMeta rim = rm.getMethodMeta(method);
7751
7752               String uri = rim.getUri();
7753               RestResponse res = null;
7754
7755               try {
7756                  RestRequest rc = request("POST", uri, true)
7757                     .serializer(serializer)
7758                     .content(args)
7759                     .rethrow(RuntimeException.class)
7760                     .rethrow(method.getExceptionTypes());
7761
7762                  res = rc.run();
7763
7764                  Object v = res.getContent().as(method.getGenericReturnType());
7765                  if (v == null && method.getReturnType().isPrimitive())
7766                     v = ClassInfo.of(method.getReturnType()).getPrimitiveDefault();
7767                  return v;
7768
7769               } catch (Throwable e) {
7770                  if (e instanceof RestCallException) {
7771                     Throwable t = e.getCause();
7772                     if (t != null)
7773                        e = t;
7774                  }
7775                  if (e instanceof RuntimeException)
7776                     throw e;
7777                  for (Class<?> t2 : method.getExceptionTypes())
7778                     if (t2.isInstance(e))
7779                        throw e;
7780                  throw runtimeException(e);
7781               }
7782            }
7783      });
7784   }
7785
7786   @Override
7787   protected void finalize() throws Throwable {
7788      if (detectLeaks && ! isClosed && ! keepHttpClientOpen) {
7789         StringBuilder sb = new StringBuilder("WARNING:  RestClient garbage collected before it was finalized.");  // NOT DEBUG
7790         if (creationStack != null) {
7791            sb.append("\nCreation Stack:");  // NOT DEBUG
7792            for (StackTraceElement e : creationStack)
7793               sb.append("\n\t" + e);  // NOT DEBUG
7794         }
7795         log(WARNING, sb.toString());
7796      }
7797   }

7799   /**
7800    * Logs a message.
7801    *
7802    * @param level The log level.
7803    * @param t Thrown exception.  Can be <jk>null</jk>.
7804    * @param msg The message.
7805    * @param args Optional message arguments.
7806    */
7807   protected void log(Level level, Throwable t, String msg, Object...args) {
7808      logger.log(level, t, msg(msg, args));
7809      if (logToConsole) {
7810         console.println(msg(msg, args).get());
7811         if (t != null)
7812            t.printStackTrace(console);
7813      }
7814   }
7815
7816   /**
7817    * Logs a message.
7818    *
7819    * @param level The log level.
7820    * @param msg The message with {@link MessageFormat}-style arguments.
7821    * @param args The arguments.
7822    */
7823   protected void log(Level level, String msg, Object...args) {
7824      logger.log(level, msg(msg, args));
7825      if (logToConsole)
7826         console.println(msg(msg, args).get());
7827   }
7828
7829   private Supplier<String> msg(String msg, Object...args) {
7830      return ()->args.length == 0 ? msg : MessageFormat.format(msg, args);
7831   }

7851   /**
7852    * Returns the part serializer instance of the specified type.
7853    *
7854    * @param c The part serializer class.
7855    * @return The part serializer.
7856    */
7857   protected HttpPartSerializer getPartSerializer(Class<? extends HttpPartSerializer> c) {
7858      HttpPartSerializer x = partSerializers.get(c);
7859      if (x == null) {
7860         try {
7861            x = beanStore.createBean(c).run();
7862         } catch (ExecutableException e) {
7863            throw runtimeException(e);
7864         }
7865         partSerializers.put(c, x);
7866      }
7867      return x;
7868   }

7871    * Returns the part parser instance of the specified type.
7872    *
7873    * @param c The part parser class.
7874    * @return The part parser.
7875    */
7876   protected HttpPartParser getPartParser(Class<? extends HttpPartParser> c) {
7877      HttpPartParser x = partParsers.get(c);
7878      if (x == null) {
7879         try {
7880            x = beanStore.createBean(c).run();
7881         } catch (ExecutableException e) {
7882            throw runtimeException(e);
7883         }
7884         partParsers.put(c, x);
7885      }
7886      return x;
7887   }

7984   /**
7985    * Interceptor method called immediately after the RestRequest object is created and all headers/query/form-data has been copied from the client.
7986    *
7987    * <p>
7988    * Subclasses can override this method to intercept the request and perform special modifications.
7989    *
7990    * <ul class='seealso'>
7991    *    <li class='jm'>{@link Builder#interceptors(Object...)}
7992    * </ul>
7993    *
7994    * @param req The HTTP request.
7995    * @throws RestCallException If any of the interceptors threw an exception.
7996    */
7997   @Override
7998   public void onInit(RestRequest req) throws RestCallException {
7999      try {
8000         for (RestCallInterceptor rci : interceptors)
8001            rci.onInit(req);
8002      } catch (RuntimeException | RestCallException e) {
8003         throw e;
8004      } catch (Exception e) {
8005         throw new RestCallException(null, e, "Interceptor threw an exception on init.");
8006      }
8007   }
8008
8009   /**
8010    * Interceptor method called immediately after an HTTP response has been received.
8011    *
8012    * <p>
8013    * Subclasses can override this method to intercept the response and perform special modifications.
8014    *
8015    * <ul class='seealso'>
8016    *    <li class='jm'>{@link Builder#interceptors(Object...)}
8017    * </ul>
8018    *
8019    * @param req The HTTP request.
8020    * @param res The HTTP response.
8021    * @throws RestCallException If any of the interceptors threw an exception.
8022    */
8023   @Override
8024   public void onConnect(RestRequest req, RestResponse res) throws RestCallException {
8025      try {
8026         for (RestCallInterceptor rci : interceptors)
8027            rci.onConnect(req, res);
8028      } catch (RuntimeException | RestCallException e) {
8029         throw e;
8030      } catch (Exception e) {
8031         throw new RestCallException(res, e, "Interceptor threw an exception on connect.");
8032      }
8033   }
8034
8035   /**
8036    * Interceptor method called immediately after the RestRequest object is created and all headers/query/form-data has been set on the request from the client.
8037    *
8038    * <p>
8039    * Subclasses can override this method to handle any cleanup operations.
8040    *
8041    * <ul class='seealso'>
8042    *    <li class='jm'>{@link Builder#interceptors(Object...)}
8043    * </ul>
8044    *
8045    * @param req The HTTP request.
8046    * @param res The HTTP response.
8047    * @throws RestCallException If any of the interceptors threw an exception.
8048    */
8049   @Override
8050   public void onClose(RestRequest req, RestResponse res) throws RestCallException {
8051      try {
8052         for (RestCallInterceptor rci : interceptors)
8053            rci.onClose(req, res);
8054      } catch (RuntimeException | RestCallException e) {
8055         throw e;
8056      } catch (Exception e) {
8057         throw new RestCallException(res, e, "Interceptor threw an exception on close.");
8058      }
8059   }

8214      return httpClient.execute(request, responseHandler);

8297
8298   private Pattern absUrlPattern = Pattern.compile("^\\w+\\:\\/\\/.*");
8299
8300   URI toURI(Object x, String rootUri) throws RestCallException {
8301      try {
8302         if (x instanceof URI)
8303            return (URI)x;
8304         if (x instanceof URL)
8305            ((URL)x).toURI();
8306         if (x instanceof URIBuilder)
8307            return ((URIBuilder)x).build();
8308         String s = x == null ? "" : x.toString();
8309         if (rootUri != null && ! absUrlPattern.matcher(s).matches()) {
8310            if (s.isEmpty())
8311               s = rootUri;
8312            else {
8313               StringBuilder sb = new StringBuilder(rootUri);
8314               if (! s.startsWith("/"))
8315                  sb.append('/');
8316               sb.append(s);
8317               s = sb.toString();
8318            }
8319         }
8320         s = fixUrl(s);
8321         return new URI(s);
8322      } catch (URISyntaxException e) {
8323         throw new RestCallException(null, e, "Invalid URI encountered:  {0}", x);  // Shouldn't happen.
8324      }
8325   }
8326
8327   ExecutorService getExecutorService() {
8328      if (executorService != null)
8329         return executorService;
8330      synchronized(this) {
8331         executorService = new ThreadPoolExecutor(1, 1, 30, TimeUnit.SECONDS, new ArrayBlockingQueue<Runnable>(10));
8332         return executorService;
8333      }
8334   }
8335
8336   /*
8337    * Returns the serializer that best matches the specified content type.
8338    * If no match found or the content type is null, returns the serializer in the list if it's a list of one.
8339    * Returns null if no serializers are defined.
8340    */
8341   Serializer getMatchingSerializer(String mediaType) {
8342      if (serializers.isEmpty())
8343         return null;
8344      if (mediaType != null) {
8345         Serializer s = serializers.getSerializer(mediaType);
8346         if (s != null)
8347            return s;
8348      }
8349      List<Serializer> l = serializers.getSerializers();
8350      return (l.size() == 1 ? l.get(0) : null);
8351   }
8352
8353   boolean hasSerializers() {
8354      return ! serializers.getSerializers().isEmpty();
8355   }
8356
8357   /*
8358    * Returns the parser that best matches the specified content type.
8359    * If no match found or the content type is null, returns the parser in the list if it's a list of one.
8360    * Returns null if no parsers are defined.
8361    */
8362   Parser getMatchingParser(String mediaType) {
8363      if (parsers.isEmpty())
8364         return null;
8365      if (mediaType != null) {
8366         Parser p = parsers.getParser(mediaType);
8367         if (p != null)
8368            return p;
8369      }
8370      List<Parser> l = parsers.getParsers();
8371      return (l.size() == 1 ? l.get(0) : null);
8372   }
8373
8374   boolean hasParsers() {
8375      return ! parsers.getParsers().isEmpty();
8376   }
8377
8378   @SuppressWarnings("unchecked")
8379   <T extends Context> T getInstance(Class<T> c) {
8380      Context o = requestContexts.get(c);
8381      if (o == null) {
8382         if (Serializer.class.isAssignableFrom(c)) {
8383            o = Serializer.createSerializerBuilder((Class<? extends Serializer>)c).beanContext(getBeanContext()).build();
8384         } else if (Parser.class.isAssignableFrom(c)) {
8385            o = Parser.createParserBuilder((Class<? extends Parser>)c).beanContext(getBeanContext()).build();
8386         }
8387         requestContexts.put(c, o);
8388      }
8389      return (T)o;
8390   }
8391
8392   private RestOperation op(String method, Object url, Object body) {
8393      return RestOperation.of(method, url, body);
8394   }
8395
8396   private Reader stringBody(String body) {
8397      return body == null ? null : new StringReader(stringify(body));
8398   }

8400   @Override /* Context */
8401   protected JsonMap properties() {
8402      return filteredMap()
8403         .append("errorCodes", errorCodes)
8404         .append("executorService", executorService)
8405         .append("executorServiceShutdownOnClose", executorServiceShutdownOnClose)
8406         .append("headerData", headerData)
8407         .append("interceptors", interceptors)
8408         .append("keepHttpClientOpen", keepHttpClientOpen)
8409         .append("partParser", partParser)
8410         .append("partSerializer", partSerializer)
8411         .append("queryData", queryData)
8412         .append("rootUri", rootUri);
8413   }
